	flavor = {
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
	}
				limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion }
				remove_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion
				trigger_event = { id = daoyu.501 popup = yes }
			}
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_target_character_mark_target_culture } remove_global_variable = daoyu_target_character_mark_target_culture trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
			else = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
		}
		else = { trigger_event = { id = dculo.20 popup = yes } }
	}
}

	option = { name = champa trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_show_cu_champa } daoyu_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "champa" } }
	option = { name = east_german trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_show_cu_east_german } daoyu_culture_effect = { CULTURE = "east_german" } }
	option = {
		name = NEXT_PAGE#下一页
		trigger = { daoyu_check_page_next = yes }
		daoyu_determine_page_next = yes
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		set_variable = daoyu_return
		random_country = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_target_country } remove_variable = daoyu_target_country }
		daoyu_remove_page_num = yes
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		default_option = yes
	}
	after = {
		daoyu_remove_show_cu_effect = yes
		if = {
			limit = { has_variable = daoyu_return }
			remove_variable = daoyu_return dculo_remove_heritage_effect = yes
			if = { limit = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_begin has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } } trigger_event = { id = dculo.20 popup = yes } }
			else = {
				dculo_remove_heritage_group_effect = yes
				if = { limit = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu has_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu } } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.510 popup = yes } }
				else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_m_cu } trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
				else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_add_homeland } remove_global_variable = daoyu_add_homeland trigger_event = { id = daoyu.572 popup = yes } }
				else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_remove_homeland } remove_global_variable = daoyu_remove_homeland trigger_event = { id = daoyu.572 popup = yes } }
			}
		}
		else = {
			if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_new_culture_for_name } daoyu_remove_page_num = yes dculo_remove_all_heritage = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu.271 popup = yes } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_target_character_mark_target_culture } daoyu_remove_page_num = yes remove_global_variable = daoyu_target_character_mark_target_culture dculo_remove_all_heritage = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_one_earth_one_nation_one_religion } daoyu_remove_page_num = yes dculo_remove_all_heritage = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu.520 popup = yes } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_mark_target_culture_complete } daoyu_remove_page_num = yes dculo_remove_all_heritage = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu.570 popup = yes } }
			else = {
				if = {
					limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu }
					if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_culture = { is_primary_culture_of = prev count > 1 } } } trigger_event = { id = dculo.30 popup = yes } }
					else = {  remove_global_variable = daoyu_r_cu daoyu_remove_page_num = yes dculo_remove_all_heritage = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { or = { has_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu has_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu } }
					if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { any_scope_culture = { not = { is_primary_culture_of = prev } count > 0 } } } trigger_event = { id = dculo.30 popup = yes } }
					else = { remove_global_variable = daoyu_a_cu remove_global_variable = daoyu_c_cu daoyu_remove_page_num = yes dculo_remove_all_heritage = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu.500 popup = yes } }
				}
				else_if = {
					limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_m_cu }
					if = { limit = { scope:daoyu_target_state = { state_is_eligible_as_mass_migration_target = yes } } trigger_event = { id = dculo.30 popup = yes } }
					else = { daoyu_remove_page_num = yes dculo_remove_all_heritage = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu.511 popup = yes } }
				}
				else = { trigger_event = { id = dculo.30 popup = yes } }
			}
		}
	}
}

#选定国家
dcc.10 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = daoyu_create_country_desc
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_country = { is_ai = yes has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID } }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_line_reaks }
		first_valid = { desc = daoyu_create_country_flavor }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = FRONTEND_SWITCH_COUNTRY#切换国家
		if = { limit = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.11 popup = yes } } }
		else = { custom_tooltip = TARGET_COUNTRY_NOT_VALID hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.10 popup = yes } } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_become_a_nonexistent_country#变身不存在的国家
		set_global_variable = daoyu_become_a_nonexistent_country
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.40 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_a_nonexistent_country_controlled_by_AI#创建由AI控制的不存在的国家
		trigger = { not = { any_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.19 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_create_a_nonexistent_country_controlled_by_AI#创建由AI控制的不存在的国家
		trigger = { any_state = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } }
		set_global_variable = dcc
		every_scope_state = { limit = { has_decree = decree_daoyu_target_state } set_variable = daoyu_potential_target set_variable = dcc_owned }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.20 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_query_countries_tag#查询国家标签
		set_variable = daoyu_query_countries_tag
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.40 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = daoyu.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#切换国家
dcc.11 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = FRONTEND_SWITCH_COUNTRY
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_root_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } desc = FRONTEND_SWITCH_COUNTRY } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = RELOAD } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } } desc = MULTIPLAYER_LOBBY_NOT_READY } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = { random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } save_scope_as = daoyu_target_country } }
	option = {
		name = NO_OBJECTIVE#你未选择目标
		trigger = { not = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.11 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_target_country#移除目标国家
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		random_country = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.11 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RELOAD#重新加载
		trigger = { any_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } scope:daoyu_target_country = { not = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.11 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = CONFIRM
		trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_treaty_articles_on } custom_tooltip = daoyu_treaty_articles_off remove_variable = daoyu_treaty_articles_on }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.12 popup = yes } }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		hidden_effect = { trigger_event = { id = dcc.10 popup = yes } }
	}
}
#切换国家
dcc.12 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	desc = FRONTEND_SWITCH_COUNTRY
	flavor = {
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_target_country } }
		first_valid = { triggered_desc = { trigger = { scope:daoyu_target_country = { has_modifier = daoyu_target_country } } desc = daoyu_target_country_get_name } }
	}
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	option = {
		name = daoyu_do_not_remove_all_modifiers#不删除修正
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_cheat
		}
		play_as = scope:daoyu_target_country
	}
	option = {
		name = daoyu_remove_all_modifiers#删除修正
		daoyu_remove_all_country_modifier_effect = yes
		daoyu_state_modifier_remove_modifier_effect = yes
		every_scope_character = {
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier } remove_modifier = daoyu_general_modifier }
			if = { limit = { has_modifier = daoyu_admiral_modifier } remove_modifier = daoyu_admiral_modifier }
		}
		hidden_effect = {
			scope:daoyu_target_country = { remove_modifier = daoyu_target_country }
			remove_global_variable = daoyu_cheat
		}
		play_as = scope:daoyu_target_country
	}
}

dcc.20 = {
	type = country_event
	placement = root
	title = daoyu_cheat
	desc = concept_capital_state
	flavor = daoyu_select_capital
	event_image = { video = "gfx/event_pictures/unspecific_signed_contract.bk2" }
	on_created_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/UI/Alerts/event_appear"
	on_opened_soundeffect = "event:/SFX/Events/unspecific/signed_contract"
	icon = "gfx/interface/icons/event_icons/event_default.dds"
	duration = 0
	immediate = {

	option = { name = 300 trigger = { has_variable = daoyu_unit_count_300 } daoyu_coe = { NUM = "300" } }
	option = {
		name = ENCYCLOPEDIAGE_NEXT_PAGE
		trigger = {
			not = { has_variable = daoyu_page_05 }
			or = {
				and = { has_variable = daoyu_page_01 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 19 }
				and = { has_variable = daoyu_page_02 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 37 }
				and = { has_variable = daoyu_page_03 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 55 }
				and = { has_variable = daoyu_page_04 var:daoyu_unit_count_var > 73 }
			}
		}
		if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_01 } remove_variable = daoyu_page_01 set_variable = daoyu_page_02 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_02 } remove_variable = daoyu_page_02 set_variable = daoyu_page_03 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_03 } remove_variable = daoyu_page_03 set_variable = daoyu_page_04 }
		else_if = { limit = { has_variable = daoyu_page_04 } remove_variable = daoyu_page_04 set_variable = daoyu_page_05 }
	}
	option = {
		name = RESIGN
		ai_chance = { base = 100 }
		set_global_variable = daoyu_220
	}
	after = {
		daoyu_unit_count_clean_effect = yes
		if = { limit = { has_global_variable = daoyu_220 } remove_global_variable = daoyu_220 trigger_event = { id = daoyu.220 popup = yes } daoyu_remove_page_num = yes }
		else_if = { limit = { daoyu_page_turning_trigger = yes } trigger_event = { id = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation.1 popup = yes } }
		else = { daoyu_remove_page_num = yes trigger_event = { id = daoyu_transfer_to_another_formation.2 popup = yes } }
	}
}
